With Exchange

Includes exchange service fee of Rs.

#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  1 Year Screen Damage Protection Plan

from Acko

[ __](/product-
reviews/B0DW9GF6L1/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0FB9DBDYP_B0DW9GF6L1?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)
[ (4) ](/product-
reviews/B0DW9GF6L1/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0FB9DBDYP_B0DW9GF6L1?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)

  * Plan is valid from the date of purchase till 1 year.
  * Plan is email delivered and auto activated if purchased along with mobile on Amazon.
  * Wear and tear, theft, accessories, intentional damages, and brand warranty exclusions are not covered
  * plan is not valid if purchased standalone.
  * How to raise a repair request: Option A: Go to Acko.com >> Enter your mobile number >> file repair. Option B: Download Acko mobile app >> Enter your mobile number >> file repair. Option C: Go to Your Orders on Amazon app >> Get Product Support >> Schedule a repair. Plan is applicable for Samsung, Mi, OnePlus, OPPO, Vivo, Realme, iQoo and Tecno phones only

##  1 Year Extended Warranty Plan

from One Assist

[ __](/product-
reviews/B0B9H84Y6S/ref=psd_bb_r2_B0FB9DBDYP_B0B9H84Y6S?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)
[ (203) ](/product-
reviews/B0B9H84Y6S/ref=psd_bb_r2_B0FB9DBDYP_B0B9H84Y6S?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)

  * Service valid when manufacturing warranty is over till the plan duration.
  * Service contract is email delivered and activated by the customer if purchased along with product on Amazon
  * Wear and tear, theft, accessories, intentional damages and brand warranty exclusions are not covered; service contract is not valid if purchased standalone

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  HONOR warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact HONOR or visit the Service Centre.
  * HONOR will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per HONOR warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

#  About this item

  * UNBREAKABLE DURABILITY :- Engineered to endure the toughest environments, this smartphone features advanced HONOR Ultra Bounce Technology and is 2-meter drop-tested by SGS. Built to be drop-resistant, heat-resistant, and water-resistant, it’s ready for any adventure—wherever life takes you. 
  * POWER THAT LASTS :- Go further without worry thanks to a massive 6600mAh Silicon Carbon Battery. With 66W SuperCharge technology, enjoy ultra-fast charging and up to 3 days of battery life, even in extreme conditions. 
  * 108MP OIS AI CAMERA :- Capture every moment in stunning detail with a 108MP OIS AI Camera. Enjoy 3x lossless zoom, AI Night Mode, and Advanced Motion Sensing for crisp, vibrant photos—day or night. 
  * EYE-COMFORT DISPLAY :- Experience next-level visuals on a 4000-nit bright, 1.5K resolution display with a 120Hz adjustable refresh rate. Designed for eye comfort, it ensures stunning clarity without strain. 
  * ULTRA-SLIM, STYLISH DESIGN :- With a sleek 7.98mm body, lightweight 189g frame, and elegant titanium finish, this phone blends high performance with a sophisticated, metallic aesthetic that stands out from the crowd. 
  * MAGIC OS POWERED BY AI :- Experience smarter, smoother interactions with AI-powered MagicOS. From intelligent app management to seamless multitasking and privacy-enhancing features, MagicOS adapts to your lifestyle for an intuitive user experience. 
  * OPERATING SYSTEM :- Experience seamless performance with MagicOS 8.0 (based on Android 14) right out of the box. Stay ahead with a future-ready upgrade to MagicOS 9.0 (based on Android 15), immediately available via OTA (Over The Air) Notification upon device activation.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers praise the phone's camera quality, describing it as super good and
robust, while also appreciating its display quality and battery life. They
find it offers good value for money, and one customer notes its smooth UI. The
charging speed receives mixed feedback, with some customers finding it very
fast while others feel it's slow.

 _5 out of 5 stars_

##### Great phone with excellent cameras

My reviews after using this phone more then 2 weeks .. Cameras are great in
this price segment.. Display ( FHD+ SMOLED with 120HZ )is very smooth cristal
clear and bright even in sunlight . POWERFUL SNAPDRAGON processor which is
capable to handle daily tasks and good performance in multitasking.. Nice
battery backup and very fast charging also .. 66 w adopter charges it under 1
hour . No heating issue till now. Dual stereo speakers are loud and clear..
Magic OS features are also very good like AI ERASER, magic portal which looks
unique.. Design is very nice , it looks so beautiful... It's a great deal on
20k price..

#####  Great phone with excellent cameras

  
Reviewed in India on 1 August 2025

My reviews after using this phone more then 2 weeks .. Cameras are great in
this price segment.. Display ( FHD+ SMOLED with 120HZ )is very smooth cristal
clear and bright even in sunlight . POWERFUL SNAPDRAGON processor which is
capable to handle daily tasks and good performance in multitasking..  
Nice battery backup and very fast charging also .. 66 w adopter charges it
under 1 hour . No heating issue till now.  
Dual stereo speakers are loud and clear..  
Magic OS features are also very good like AI ERASER, magic portal which looks
unique..  
Design is very nice , it looks so beautiful... It's a great deal on 20k
price..
